        '/**\r\n' +
        ' * @dev Standard INFT_DB decentralized database for custodial NFTs for customers.\r\n' +

        'contract standardNFT_DB is\r\n' +

        '    ERC165Upgradeable,\r\n' +
        '    ERC1155PausableUpgradeable,\r\n' +
        '    ReentrancyGuardUpgradeable,\r\n' +

        '\r\n' +
        '    string private _contractLevelMetadataURI; //See https://docs.opensea.io/docs/contract-level-metadata\r\n' +
        '\r\n' +
        '    mapping(uint256 => string) private _tokenURIs; //tokenURI custom implementation\r\n' +
        '\r\n' +
        '    mapping(uint256 => bool) private tokenMinted; //Check if tokenID has already been minted\r\n' +
        '    mapping(uint256 => bool) private isBurnable; //Check if tokenID is burnable\r\n' +
        '    mapping(uint256 => bool) private isMutable; //Check if tokenID URI is mutable, if his URI can be changed at a later time\r\n' +
        '\r\n' +
        '    //Metadata variables declaration\r\n' +
        '    string public name;\r\n' +
        '\r\n' +
        '    function initialize(\r\n' +
        '        string memory contract_uri,\r\n' +
        '        address[] memory admins,\r\n' +
        '        string memory contract_name\r\n' +
        '    ) public initializer {\r\n' +
        '        //Dependencies initialization:\r\n' +
        '        __ERC1155_init(contract_uri);\r\n' +
        '        __ReentrancyGuard_init();\r\n' +
        '\r\n' +
        '        //Contract variables setup\r\n' +
        '        _contractLevelMetadataURI = contract_uri;\r\n' +
        '        name = contract_name;\r\n' +
        '\r\n' +
        '        if (admins.length > 0) {\r\n' +
        '            //first admin assignation\r\n' +
        '            for (uint256 i = 0; i < admins.length; i++) {\r\n' +
        '                _grantRole(DEFAULT_ADMIN_ROLE, admins[i]);\r\n' +
        '            }\r\n' +
        '        }\r\n' +
        '    }\r\n' +
        '\r\n' +
        '    /**\r\n' +
        '     * @dev uri function override, allows to assign a custom URI for each token ID\r\n' +
        '     *\r\n' +
        '     * @param tokenId: uint, token id of which we want to get the URI set by _SetTokenURI\r\n' +
        '     * @return URI: string, URI address of tokenId token\r\n' +
        '     */\r\n' +
        '    function uri(uint256 tokenId) public view override returns (string memory) {\r\n' +
        '        require(_exists(tokenId), "ERC1155: query for non-existent object");\r\n' +
        '        return (_tokenURIs[tokenId]);\r\n' +
        '    }\r\n' +
        '\r\n' +
        '    /**\r\n' +
        '     * @dev return custom collection URI, for legacy purposes\r\n' +
        '     *\r\n' +
        '     * @return _contractLevelMetadataURI: string, the contract URI assigned from the constructor\r\n' +
        '     */\r\n' +
        '    function tokenURI() public view returns (string memory) {\r\n' +
        '        return _contractLevelMetadataURI;\r\n' +
        '    }\r\n' +
        '\r\n' +
        '    /**\r\n' +
        '     * @dev Utility string comparation function. Allows to check if a and b are equal.\r\n' +
        '     *\r\n' +
        '     * @param a: string, the first string to compare\r\n' +
        '     * @param b: string, the second string to compare\r\n' +
        '     * @return equals: bool, says if a and b are equal\r\n' +
        '     */\r\n' +
        '    function compareStrings(string memory a, string memory b)\r\n' +
        '        public\r\n' +
        '        pure\r\n' +
        '        returns (bool)\r\n' +
        '    {\r\n' +
        '        return keccak256(abi.encodePacked(a)) == keccak256(abi.encodePacked(b));\r\n' +
        '    }\r\n' +
        '\r\n' +
        '    function contractURI() public view returns (string memory) {\r\n' +
        '        return _contractLevelMetadataURI;\r\n' +
        '    }\r\n' +
        '\r\n' +
        '    function mintToken(\r\n' +
        '        address to,\r\n' +
        '        uint256 tokenId,\r\n' +
        '        uint256 amount,\r\n' +
        '        string memory contract_uri,\r\n' +
        '        bool burnable,\r\n' +
        '        bool nonMutable\r\n' +
        '    ) public nonReentrant onlyRole(ADMIN_ROLE) {\r\n' +
        '        if (_exists(tokenId)) {\r\n' +
        '            _mint(to, tokenId, amount, "");\r\n' +
        '        }\r\n' +
        '        //if it exist already, just mintToken the NFT\r\n' +
        '        else {\r\n' +
        '            _mint(to, tokenId, amount, "");\r\n' +
        '            tokenMinted[tokenId] = true;\r\n' +
        '            _setTokenUri(tokenId, contract_uri); //if token URI is empty, token is considered ERC20 like\r\n' +
        '\r\n' +
        '            //allows users to block current token burn. this is permanent.\r\n' +
        '            if (burnable) {\r\n' +
        '                isBurnable[tokenId] = true;\r\n' +
        '            }\r\n' +
        '\r\n' +
        '            //allows customers to avoid tokenURI changes\r\n' +
        '            if (!nonMutable) {\r\n' +
        '                isMutable[tokenId] = false;\r\n' +
